HINT DB3 = switch or actuator
HINT CF  = Cell flags
HINT L   = dungeon level
HINT TX  = target X
HINT TY  = target Y
HINT TP  = target position
HINT OO  = once only
HINT au  = audible
HINT NC  = normally closed
HINT NO  = normally open
HINT DL  = delay
HINT act = action
HINT LK  = link (pos,db,index)
HINT obj = object (pos,db,index)
HINT disable = #clock ticks monster generator is disabled
HINT num = number of monsters to generate
